			1. pUrNawvakAmanA

SENT:  yaH yasmAw jAyawe saH api svapiwA iva buBURawi
ANALYSIS:

2 yasmAw apAxAnam 3
3 jAyawe 
4 saH karwA 8
5 api sambanXaH 4
6 svapiwA prawiyogI 7
7 iva anuyogI 4
8 buBURawi

SENT:  nahi sUryoxBavaH vahniH SIwaH Bavawi vArivaw 
ANALYSIS:

3 vahniH karwA 5 
4 SIwaH karwqsamAnAXikaraNam 5
5 Bavawi
6 vArivaw kriyAviSeRaNam 5

SENT: 2 ekA gqhiNI svasya pawye Bojane ekaM pUrNaM moxakaM puwrAya ca arXaM moxakaM paryaveRayaw

SENT:  (jIvAwmA) aMSarUpeNa sWAwuM na icCawi iwi

				103. sarvaH sarvaM na prApnowi
			sarvaM samIhiwaM sarvaH+ na+eva+Apnowi kaxAcana
			kaScana BAgyaSAlI+eva, laBawe svaM samIhiwam

SENT:  saMyukwaparivAre prawisaxasyaM vicAraXArAyAH BinnaBinnawvAw parasparaM maXye maXye kalahaH asahayogaH ca svABAvikaH eva (aswi)

5. buxXimAn svakAryaM kaWaM sAXayawi ?
